## "Chant Anyway" by Srila Bhaktivinod Thakur | Soulful Japa
**Speaker:** HDG Srila Prabhupada

### chanting, obstacles, holy name
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/N9FXMsAY_50?t=0
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers, Newcomers, General public
**Key Quote:** "You are making offenses in chanting. Chant anyway."
**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada quotes Bhaktivinoda Thakur, emphasizing the importance of chanting the Hare Krishna mantra regardless of any obstacles or imperfections in one's practice.

I will put one writing of Bhaktivinoda Thakur. You read that. Then you will see how we should be towards, how our attitude should be towards the general population chanting Hare Krishna. This is Bhaktivinoda Thakur's Sharanagati quoted from Adi Purana. It's called chant anyway. It starts like this: Your mind is wandering all over the universe when you chant. Chant anyway. Your mind is wandering to the past and future when you chant. Chant anyway. You are not able to concentrate on Krishna's names while you chant. Chant anyway. You have no taste for chanting. Chant anyway. You have lusty desires. Chant anyway. You are making offenses in chanting. Chant anyway. You are not praying to Krishna to help you chant better. Chant anyway.

### holy name, liberation, devotion
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/N9FXMsAY_50?t=59
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers, Newcomers, General public
**Key Quote:** "There is no vow like chanting the Holy Name. There's no knowledge superior to it."
**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada continues quoting Bhaktivinoda Thakur, explaining the unparalleled benefits of chanting the holy name, highlighting its power to grant liberation, peace, and eternal life.

You often chant late at night. Chant anyway. And why, why should you chant despite all the above obstacles? That is why. What is that? There is no vow like chanting the Holy Name. There's no knowledge superior to it. There is no meditation which comes anywhere near it and it gives the highest result. No penance is equal to it and nothing is as potent or powerful as the holy name. Chanting is the greatest act of piety and the supreme refuge. Even the words of Vedas do not possess sufficient power to describe its magnitude. It's continuing chanting is the highest path to liberation, peace, and eternal life. It's a pinnacle of devotion, heart's joyous proclivity and attraction. See it's a joyous heart's joyous proclivity and attraction and the best form of remembrance of the Supreme Lord.

**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada emphasizes that the holy name is for the benefit of all living entities and that continuous chanting, even in sleep, leads to the realization that the name is a direct manifestation of Krishna.

The holy name has appeared solely for the benefit of all living entities as their lord and master, nama prabhu, their supreme worshipable object and their spiritual guide and mentor who are continuously chants Lord Krishna's holy name even in his sleep can easily realize that the name is a direct manifestation of Krishna himself.

There was one devotee named Guru Kripa. He was Swami Aditya. He went to Prabhupada. He says, "Prabhupada, of all the things that you have taught, what is the most important?" And Prabhupada says, "That if you have firm faith in Guru and Krishna, then everything will be revealed to you."

### obedience, guru, mental speculation
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/9rU41b2J7qs?t=83
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees
**Key Quote:** "But we see that so-called higher understanding is not based on the law book of ISKCON. It is based on Manodharma."
**Summary:** The speaker argues that Prabhupada's books were appreciated by scholars and that the claim of a 'higher understanding' justifying changes is based on mental speculation (Manodharma), not the established principles of ISKCON.

When Prabhupada was there, there were so many scholars. You read this Bhagavad Gita. So many scholars have given nice reviews and appreciation of his books. Amir Velas Maharaj knows he was there. You see? So many scholars would come. Did any one of them complain? Oh, no. This is not proper. None of them would dare do that. They all appreciate it. Prabhupada has given no such instruction that you go rewrite all the books. Of course, those who claim that they have seen the truth, they have so-called higher understanding. But we see that so-called higher understanding is not based on the law book of ISKCON. It is based on Manodharma. Manodharma in Chaitanya Charitam is described as mental speculation. He concocts something out of the thin air. Manodharma.

Actually, in 1969, one devotee asked Prabhupada the question, what happens after the spiritual master departs, because the spiritual master, he says, he will deliver all the disciples. Prabhupada said, "I remain in the universe as long as all my disciples are not delivered." So this idea that Guru is dead and gone, this is Gnastika. You all know Hindi or Sanskrit, some Sanskrit, not Gnastika, that means this is atheist philosophy. Some time ago, we had some disputation with some of our brothers in San Diego, California in 1990, and one of such less intelligent people says, "Oh, why don't you send a letter to Prabhupada and tell us what he replies?" Actually, this is Aparaj, but the reason we are repeating this is, first of all, that was made directly in front of Aditya Prabhupada, which just shows the ignorance of the people. So my reply is basically, I'm not going to tell you anything. I say, well, why don't you offer Krishna some prasadam, and after 15 minutes, why don't you see if it's still there? So if it's still there, do you conclude there's no Krishna? So all these arguments about living, this is actually due to a poor fund of knowledge.

## 063  Srila Prabhupada is the Summum bonum of all acharyas
**Speaker:** HDG Srila Prabhupada

### hospitality, Vaishnava culture, Chaitanya Mahaprabhu
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/rgFgDCnVDM0?t=0
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** story
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "Your Mahaprabhu came to this house."
**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada narrates an experience in Sri Rangam where they were initially denied entry to the temple but were later welcomed by a Brahmin who was a descendant of Gopal Bhattagoswami and a devotee of Chaitanya Mahaprabhu.

What is the essence of all Shastra? The Prophet has taught the essence of all Shastra. One time we went to Sri Rangam. There used to be... Actually, when we first came to Sri Rangam, there was... They had a sign there, 'Non-Hindus Allowed.' There was one life member in Shishadipuram. He sent his car with us. So we went to Sri Rangam, and we did not know we were Westerners. So we tried to go over to Darshanam. He says, 'No, Non-Hindus Allowed. You are Mleches. You cannot go.' The only person who can let you in is this Archaka, this Rangaraj Bhatta. Rangaraj Bhatta at that time was the chief Archaka of the Sri Rangam temple. So where does he live? Since we went there. So we see this Brahmin, big, big Brahmin. Oh, very big. Must have been... He comes out of his house. He says, 'Oh, you have come.' We did not know him. He offered his obeisances. He says, 'Come inside.' First thing we see inside, there's a picture of Chaitanya Mahaprabhu. He says, 'What is this picture?' 'Oh, we are descendants of Gopal Bhattagoswami.' 'Really?' 'Oh, yeah. He lived... Your Mahaprabhu came to this house.' Actually, when Chaitanya Mahaprabhu visited Sri Rangam in about 1514, something like that, he stayed in that house to observe Chaturmasya. Very old house. So they worshipped Mahaprabhu. They worshipped Chaturmasya. They worshipped Mahaprabhu on the wall. They are direct descendants of the relatives of Gopal Bhattag. And he told us... Then he says, 'I will show you another deity.' He took us to another little street there. And they have very old Jagannath deities that Chaitanya Mahaprabhu worshipped when he was in Jagannath Puri. So then he sat us down. And he brought us to the temple. And he, of course, he spoke very good Tamil. And he chastised them, chastised the Brahmins. 'No, no, let them, let them.' Then he brought us. And we had the darshan of Lord Ranganath and everything.

### translation, devotional ecstasy, commentaries
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/rgFgDCnVDM0?t=148
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees
**Key Quote:** "These books are my devotional ecstasies."
**Summary:** The Brahmin explains that Prabhupada's greatness lies in his ability to understand and synthesize the commentaries of various Vaishnava acharyas. Prabhupada's translation process is described as a deep analysis of numerous commentaries, resulting in purports that capture the essence of all the acharyas. Prabhupada emphasizes that his books are not just translations but expressions of his devotional ecstasies.

And we asked him, how do you say that? He says, because in order to do this, you not only do you have to know Sanskrit, but you have to know just not the Sanskrit. You have to be able to read all the commentaries of the acharyas. Just what we read today. Actually, when Prabhupada was here a few times, we had the chance at night in 1977 to watch Prabhupada translate the book. And he had this big, big book. It must have been like, it's a huge book that was published 200 years ago. It has all the Sanskrit commentaries of all the Vaishnava acharyas. It has the commentary of Vijaya Advaita. It has the commentary of the Vedic scriptures. It has the commentary of the Vedic literature. It has the commentary of the Madhva Sampradaya. It has the commentary of the Viragavacharya of the Sri Sampradaya. It has the commentary of the Vala Bhacharyas. It has the commentary of the Jiva Goswami. It has the commentary of the Sanatana Goswami. It has the commentary of the Prophet's Guru, Bhaktisiddhanta's commentary, Bhaktivinoda Thakur's commentary. So many commentaries all in Sanskrit. In order to produce these, you know, 25, 26 lines, the Prophet would sometimes take an hour and he's analyzing all of this. And he's giving these purports. So these purports of all the essence of all these Acharyas. Another time, one devotee asked, 'O Prophet, why don't you translate faster? We want to publish more books quicker, quicker.' The Prophet says, 'You do not understand. You do not understand.' He says, 'These books are my devotional ecstasies.'

## 072  Why Srila Prabhupada preached atheists
**Speaker:** HDG Srila Prabhupada

### karma, sin, atheism, punishment
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/JKoV50GOuR8?t=0
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "For such people, the punishment is the most severe."
**Summary:** The speaker explains that the severity of punishment for sinful acts depends on the level of awareness and belief in God, with atheism leading to the most severe consequences.

You see, the same act performed by a person who is completely ignorant, the resultant punishment is least severe. And if somebody knows the difference between what is pious and impious activity, still performs the impious activity, then his punishment is more severe. But the most severe punishment is given to one who performs sinful activities out of atheism. I don't care for God. There is no God. There is no next life. For such people, the punishment is the most severe.

---

That is why the Acharyas, they show compassion upon such people who are acting out of atheism, and try to preach Krishna consciousness among such atheists. Otherwise, to preach Krishna consciousness among atheists is the most difficult. They simply argue in various ways and they challenge and they mock and ridicule and even harm devotees. They become envious. They become more envious when you try to preach to them.

**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/JKoV50GOuR8?t=82
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** story
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "But still, he did not actually take offense."
**Summary:** The speaker narrates the story of Nithyananda Prabhu preaching to sinful and envious people, specifically at Jagayan Madai, and how he was attacked for his efforts, yet remained merciful and did not take offense.

This is Nithyananda Prabhu. He was preaching about chanting. And he even went to this Jagayan Madai, who were completely sinful and also envious of devotees. But still, Nithyananda Prabhu went to them and preached to them to save them. And in return for his trying to help them or save them, what did he get? He was attacked. And he started bleeding. But still, he did not actually take offense. This is the unlimited, causeless mercy of Lord Nithyananda.

## 096  Srila Prabhupada's is parampara understanding of philosophy
**Speaker:** HDG Srila Prabhupada

### parampara, envy, self-realization, householder life
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/bLUgYC-iRho?t=7
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "Prabhupada is giving the parampara understanding."
**Summary:** The speaker explains how Srila Prabhupada translates with the parampara understanding, using the example of 'envious householder' to illustrate the difference between a grahamedhi and a grahasta.

What is the condition of people in general? There are so many subject matters for discussing, but they don't discuss about Krishna because they are blind to self-realization. Why? Because they are attached to happy home, family life. And their time in family life is spent away both day and night in some activities which have no spiritual benefit. The lifetime, Prabhupada translates this verse as the lifetime of such an envious householder. He doesn't say just householder. So when we were translating or getting it translated this English to Kannada, the Bhagavatam, one translator objected to this. He says where in the verse, Sanskrit verse, it is said envious householder. He doesn't say envious householder. The word envy is not used in Sanskrit. Why is Prabhupada telling envious householder? So there is a mistake in the translation or there is some problem here. Actually, Prabhupada translates not just literally always. Prabhupada is giving the parampara understanding. The parampara understanding. You should not forget that. Prabhupada is not just taking the Sanskrit and writing the English. No. He is giving the parampara understanding. The Acharyas explain how a householder who is blind to self-realization, who is attached to family life, is an envious person. Elsewhere, Prabhupada says what is the difference between a grahamedhi and a grahasta? Grahamedhi is explained as an envious householder. Envious householder. Because such a person is busy always with his limited self-interest. What is the self, conception of the self? I am the body and my bodily connections are mine. Aham ameti. This is the conception of the householder who is blind to self-realization, who is materially attached to family life. Therefore such a person is described as an envious householder. So this translation says the lifetime of such an envious householder is passed at night either in sleeping or in sex indulgence. Bhagavatam is very strong.

### offering, devotion, love
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/OCAkGM6MIsQ?t=0
**Verse References:** BG 9.26
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers, Newcomers
**Key Quote:** "What Krishna is really looking at is the feeling with which we are offering, the devotion with which we are offering."
**Summary:** We should always bring an offering to the temple, even something small like a leaf, water, or fruit, but more importantly, it should be offered with love and devotion.

Pravupada also mentions that whenever we go to the temple, we are going to meet the Supreme Personality of Godhead, and we should take something, some gifts or presents or some offering to the Supreme Personality of Godhead. We should never go empty-handed. That is why we see generally in all the temples there is a custom that whenever devotees go, they bring something, some flower, some fruit. Krishna is not expecting a big offering from us. Krishna says in Bhagavad Gita, "You can offer him a leaf, water, or a fruit." These things are very easy to get. We don't need to possess a lot of wealth or money. It is easily obtainable. But more than even this, what Krishna is really looking at is the feeling with which we are offering, the devotion with which we are offering.

We offer something very best, something very precious to our parents, right? And we have no issues about that. Rather we will be very happy. ### offering, ownership, devotion
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/OCAkGM6MIsQ?t=95
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "Everything belongs to the Lord, and I am only offering it back to the Lord."
**Summary:** Everything we have comes from Krishna, so our offerings are really just returning what already belongs to Him.

And everything that I have got is from my father. So actually our offering to the Supreme Personality of Godhead, in the strictest sense, is not really an offering from us. It is the Lord's own wealth, the Lord's own profit. Everything belongs to the Lord, and I am only offering it back to the Lord. And the Lord also actually is not in need of any offering, per se.

### love, devotion, offering
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/OCAkGM6MIsQ?t=121
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers, Newcomers
**Key Quote:** "He is just looking for that love and devotion."
**Summary:** Krishna is self-sufficient and doesn't need our offerings, but He eagerly accepts the love and devotion with which we offer them, as illustrated by Sudama's offering of chipped rice.

He is self-sufficient. He is Swarat. He doesn't need anything. He has hundreds and thousands of servants, and he has all the opulences. Aishwarya, one of the qualities of the Supreme Personality of God is Aishwarya. He has enough of everything. But he is just looking for that love and devotion. A small little bit of offering that we give to him with love and devotion. He is more eager to take that than anything else. Just like Sudama, he got chipped rice. It is considered to be something very insignificant for Krishna, who is the King of Dwarka. But he relished that because Sudama brought it with love and devotion. So this is how we offer to Krishna, with love and devotion, whatever best we have, we can offer.

## 181  Srila Prabhupada claims that he is the representative of God
**Speaker:** HDG Srila Prabhupada

### Guru, Representative of God, Spiritual Vision
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/jJ7C3r3Tv6c?t=0
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "So there is no doubt about it that I am the representative of God."
**Summary:** A devotee recounts a dream where he saw a representative of God, and Srila Prabhupada confirms that he is that representative, citing scriptural support for the Guru being a manifestation of God.

There was one conversation, one devotee came to Prabhupada and he said, "They are telling me that you are going to see the representative of God. And when I came to that vision, I saw the person. At that time, I didn't know who he was, but I had some doubts in my mind and I was thinking, 'Oh, that's probably another kind of propaganda.' This was all in the dream. But when I came to that person sitting on the elevated seat in that forest, surrounded by many, many devotees, that person looked at me and proved to me that he was representative of God." So this person, devotee, was telling that I had a dream. And in the dream, there was a representative of God surrounded by many, many devotees, and he looked at me and proved that he was representative of God. But after that, I forgot. Maybe one year or something like that, one or two years after. Prabhupada, then Prabhupada replies, "So there is no doubt about it that I am the representative of God." So this devotee is saying, "I had a dream, representative of God was there, many devotees were there." So Prabhupada says, "There is no doubt about it that I am the representative of God." The devotee says, "Yes, but when I was..." Prabhupada, "Either you dream or not dream, I claim that I am representative." "Because I had a dream and some person was there, something similar to you. So therefore, you are a representative of God." Prabhupada says, "Whether you dream or you don't dream, I am claiming that I am representative of God." Prabhupada says, "Yes, but this thing was just confirming. When I saw you the first time in Amsterdam, you were the same person that I saw in my dream one or two years previously." Prabhupada says, "You have read Chaitanya Charita Amrita, Guru Tattva. So there is clearly said that Guru is the manifestation of God. So it is confirmed. So it is confirmed in the Shastra and all the Acharyas accept it. Yasya Prasadat Bhagwat Prasad."

Very tiny children without any energy, we don't have spiritual energy now to follow all the rules and regulations strictly, we are impelled by Maya's illusions and somehow we came in touch with a pure devotee like Srila Prabhupada who has taken the responsibility of delivering anyone who has come in touch with him. Can you see what a greatest service he is doing to the mankind? He has come from the spiritual world to please the Supreme Lord by delivering millions and millions of fallen souls of Kali Yuga for the next 10,000 years. So such a great responsibility Srila Prabhupada has taken. You can just imagine how fallen we all are. We are all coming from all sorts of sinful backgrounds and we are all rotting in this material world. And just by coming in touch with Srila Prabhupada's instructions, his shelter, we are really relieved from Maya's torture and we have a hope of going back to God just by following Srila Prabhupada's instructions. He is the only hope for us, there is no other link for us between us and Krishna. He is the only person because he is the only person who is able to tell us, "You do this, you don't do this." Or else if you take scriptures on our own, you will not be able to do this. If you take scriptures on your own and try to read, you will be fully confused. We don't know what to follow and what not to follow, it's totally confusing. So without the help of a spiritual master, it's impossible to go back to Godhead. So it is our duty to somehow or other stick to the instructions given by Guru and then execute it to the best of our ability. In this way we will be able to overcome Maya's influence and we will come back to our normal condition. Thank you.

## Can We Serve Krishna in Our Own Way? | HDG Srila Prabhupada | Bg 1.45-46 | 03.08.2024
**Speaker:** HDG Srila Prabhupada

### Arjuna's Dilemma, Duty, Compassion
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/h8hMfQp6ZFs?t=0
**Verse References:** BG 1.45, BG 1.46
**Content Type:** story
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "Arjuna, having thus spoken on the battlefield, cast aside his bow and arrows and sat down on the chariot, his mind overwhelmed with grief."
**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada reads and explains verses 45 and 46 from the first chapter of Bhagavad-gita, describing Arjuna's reluctance to fight and his overwhelming grief.

OM NAMO BHAGAVATE VASUDEVAYA. Reading from Srimad Bhagavad Gita, Chapter 1, entitled, Observing the Army on the Battlefield of Kuruksetra, Verse No. 45: YADIMAM APRATITARAM ASASTRAM SASTRA PANAYAH DATARASTRA RANIHANYOS TANME SHEMATARAM BHAVET. Translation and Purport by His Divine Grace A.C. Bhaktivedanta Swami Srila Prabhupada: I would consider it better for the sons of Dhritarashtra to kill me unarmed and unresisting rather than fight with them. Purport by His Grace A.C. Bhaktivedanta Swami Srila Prabhupada: It is a custom according to Kshatriya fighting principles that unarmed and unwilling foe should not be attacked. Arjuna, however, in such an enigmatic position, decided he would not fight if he were attacked. He did not consider how much the other party was bent upon fighting. All these symptoms are due to soft-heartedness resulting from his being a great devotee of the Lord. Verse No. 46. I will read myself. Sanjaya uvacha evam uttvarjunasankhe rathopastupa visat visrajya sasaramchapam sotra samvitnam anasah. Translation: Sanjaya said, Arjuna, having thus fought on the battlefield, tossed aside his bow and arrows and sat down on the chariot, his mind overwhelmed with grief. Perfect. While observing the situation of his enemy, Arjuna stood up on the chariot, but he was so afflicted, he pleaded with lamentation that he sat down again, setting aside his bow and arrows. Such a trained and soft-hearted person in the devotional service of the Lord is fit to receive self-knowledge. I would consider it better for the sons of Dhritarashtra to kill me unarmed and unresisting rather than fight with them. Sanjaya said, Arjuna, having thus spoken on the battlefield, cast aside his bow and arrows and sat down on the chariot, his mind overwhelmed with grief.

### Kshatriya Dharma, Surrender, Krishna's Order
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/h8hMfQp6ZFs?t=192
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "You can violate the laws on the order of Kṛṣṇa. This is surrender."
**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada explains the rules of kshatriya warfare and how they can be superseded by the order of Krishna, emphasizing the importance of surrender.

yadimam apratikaram asastram sastra-pāṇaya. It is the custom between the kṣatriyas, that in the fighting, if the other party hasn't got weapon to fight, this party will supply him weapon. Note that the other party without weapon and this party will take opportunity to kill him. This is not the rules and regulation of fighting. There are many rules and regulations of the fighting. Not that because he's my enemy, I shall kill him anyway. No. There are rules and regulations. If the enemy has broken his chariot, he's fallen down on the ground, he's been killed. The other party also will immediately get down from the chariot. Suppose he is fleeing, then if one is on the foot and another on the chariot, so he will be in superior position. Therefore the opposite party must also get down from the chariot and walk with him. That means the defeated enemy should be given all opportunities. So he may not think that unnecessarily, in weak position, he has been killed. No. So Arjuna says… Arjuna, of course, did later on. When he killed Karna, Karna was without weapon, and he fell down from the chariot. Karna, after falling down from the chariot, and he was trying to raise the wheel of the chariot from the mud. So Kṛṣṇa asked Arjuna that this is the opportunity to kill him. You kill him immediately. So at that time he had no weapons, and he was trying to kill Karna, and he fell down from the chariot. And in that position he was killed by Arjuna, by the order of Kṛṣṇa. This is violating the laws. So you can violate the laws on the order of Kṛṣṇa. You cannot do. This is surrender.

### Surrender, Truthfulness, Krishna's Pleasure
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/h8hMfQp6ZFs?t=386
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "My principle should be, if Kṛṣṇa is satisfied, then everything is all right."
**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada continues discussing surrender to Krishna, using the example of Yudhisthira Maharaja and emphasizing that pleasing Krishna is the ultimate goal, even if it appears wrong from a mundane perspective.

When Kṛṣṇa says that you do this, although it is wrong, you have to surrender. You cannot do that. You cannot do that. You cannot do that. You cannot do that. You cannot do that. You cannot do that. You cannot do that. You cannot do it. There is no consideration. Just like in fight the commander says to the soldiers, do this. His duty is to do that. He should not think at that time what is right or wrong. Just like Yudhiṣṭhira Mahārāja… He was advised by Kṛṣṇa that Yudhiṣṭhira, you go to Dronācārya and inform him that your son is dead. It was a false information. Because Dronācārya will not die if he is not affected with some lamentation. So Kṛṣṇa asked Mahārāja Yudhiṣṭhira that you go, because you were recognized truthful, dharma-rāja. So when he will say this is also false, he will believe. But Yudhiṣṭhira hesitated. How can I tell lie? He disobeyed the order of Kṛṣṇa. And he wanted to become very truthful. For this reason, he had to see hell. So in the mundane consideration, there are so many things, right and wrong. So long you are on the mundane platform, you have to obey all these right and wrong. But in the spiritual world, you have to obey all these right and wrong. But in the spiritual platform, when it is ordered by Kṛṣṇa, He is above all these duality. He is absolute. So even if He says to do something wrong, because He cannot say anything which is wrong, God is all good. If you discriminate God's order from the mundane platform, then you will be misguided. Anyone who has got formed and fixed up faith that whatever God does, whatever God orders, even from mundane calculation it may be wrong, that is right. That is absolute understanding. So those who are in the spiritual platform, for them, there is no such consideration which is right and which is wrong. Their only consideration is whether Kṛṣṇa is pleased. That's all. If Kṛṣṇa is pleased, by inducing me to do something wrong, I will not hesitate to do it. I shall do it. Because it's Kṛṣṇa. It's Kṛṣṇa's order.

---
### Spiritual Authority, Discernment, Guidance
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/h8hMfQp6ZFs?t=589
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers, Newcomers
**Key Quote:** "You have to get it confirmed from the transparent medium, spiritual master."
**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada warns against concocting ideas about pleasing Krishna on the mundane platform and emphasizes the need for guidance from a spiritual master.

My principle should be, if Kṛṣṇa is satisfied, then everything is all right. But while we are in the mundane platform, we should not concoct the idea that Kṛṣṇa is pleased. Let me do that. No. That you cannot do. You have to follow the rules and regulations. But if you think that it is... You cannot think. Neither you can manufacture. So either you should hear from directly, from Kṛṣṇa directly, or that is not possible because we are not in touch with Kṛṣṇa at the present moment. We are trying to see Kṛṣṇa through the transparent medium of spirituality. So we cannot manufacture that this is Kṛṣṇa's desire. No. You have to get it confirmed from the transparent medium, spiritual master. These are the principles.

### Arjuna's Reasoning, Non-Violence, Krishna's Plan
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/h8hMfQp6ZFs?t=664
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "If you think that I don't fight, that they will take the opportunity and kill me immediately, that also I shall prefer. But I am not going to fight."
**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada returns to the verses from Bhagavad-gita, explaining Arjuna's reasoning for not wanting to fight, even if it means being killed.

So Arjuna says, yadimāṁ apratikāraṁ. Pratikāraṁ apratikāraṁ. Pratikāraṁ means counteraction. And apratikāraṁ means without any counteraction. So he is informing Kṛṣṇa, that if the other party, dhārta-rāśrā, the sons of Dhrtarāśrā, other party, they kill me while I am not prepared, but that is not the regulation of fighting. So therefore he says, apratikāraṁ. If I am not prepared and they kill me, all of a sudden. This is wrong. So I accept, even they kill me, apratikāraṁ, without I am fully equipped. Asastraṁ. In the fight, one must be equipped with all, all weapons. But while I am not equipped with weapons, or I am not willing to fight, because I am not willing to fight, this has been decided. I cannot kill my kinsmen. Therefore, I am not going to take the step of pratikāraṁ, counteraction. So even in this condition, they come and kill me. Yadimāṁ apratikāraṁ asastraṁ. I am not fully equipped with asa-sastra, weapons. Asastraṁ and sastra-pāṇayaṁ, they are fully equipped with weapons. Rās-rās-rās, rane, hanyu. So in this condition, the other party, my cousin brothers, sons of the rās-rās, if they kill me, rane, hanyu, I shall prefer them. I am not going to fight. If you think that if you don't fight, then they will take the opportunity. He is talking with Kṛṣṇa. He is already giving the counter-argument. Kṛṣṇa, if you think that I don't fight, that they will take the opportunity and kill me immediately, that also I shall prefer. But I am not going to fight. But I am not going to fight. But I am not going to fight. But I am not going to fight. This is my decision.

### Material World, Danger, Counteraction

**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada explains the concept of 'pratikaram' (counteraction) in the material world, where danger is present at every step, and the need to find ways to protect oneself.

So apratikāraṁ pratikāraṁ. There are two things. Pratikāraṁ means counteraction. Here in this material world, for everything there is counteraction. Just like if you are diseased, so you have to take the medicine. Pratikāraṁ. That is pratikāraṁ. The disease is caused by some, what is called, disarrangement within the body. So we have to arrange, we have to set up the disarrangement within the body. That is pratikāraṁ, medicine, counteraction. Similarly, if somebody is diseased, he has to take the medicine. If somebody is coming to kill you, so you also become prepared to kill him. This is pratikāraṁ. If somebody is drowning in the sea, then you have to give him some help, send some boat or some lifebuoy so that he can be saved. So we have got so many. This material world is going on. It is full of dangers. Yes. Padam padam yata vipadam. Material world means step by step, simply danger. That is material world. So you have to find out pratikāraṁ, counteraction, how to save yourself from danger. Just like when we walk, we see in so many doors, danger. So that you may be, you are warned. Sometimes the doors are, beware of the door. So you have to take care. No, I shall not enter. So everything, there is danger and there is pratikāraṁ, counter, counteraction, how to save yourself from this. This is called struggle for existence. In this material world...

Anyone who has taken shelter of the lotus feet of Kṛṣṇa. Samāsthita ye pada-pallavam plavam. Mahat-padam kurna-jaso murāre. Murāre, murāre means Kṛṣṇa. So purna-jaso is simply glorified by pious activities. There is no impious activities in Kṛṣṇa. Kṛṣṇa is the purest. So whatever he does, that is pure. The rascals, they do not know this. You do not know something. Perfectly, and still you are talking about it. This is going on. Purna-jaso murāre. What is Kṛṣṇa? Kṛṣṇa says, bholam janmalā mante jñānavāṁ mām kṛpady. We have to know Kṛṣṇa. Because as soon as you know Kṛṣṇa, you become immediately independent. So knowing Kṛṣṇa is not so easy thing. Therefore Kṛṣṇa says, manuṣyānāṁ śahaśreṣu kaścid yatati siddhayaḥ. First of all, you become siddha, perfect. Perfect means perfect knowledge. That is called siddha. And another siddha means very powerful, master of all yogic perfection. That is also siddha. Yogi is perfection, eight kinds of perfection. Manimā, lagimā, siddhi, prapti, yasitā, bhashitā, prāpaṁ mam. So they update eight kinds of siddhis. They are also called siddhas. From material point of view, a perfect yogi can counteract anything, and whatever he likes, he can do. That is called siddhi, astra-siddhi. But still, he is not as siddha as Kṛṣṇa. Kṛṣṇa's name is yogi-śara. He is the master of all the yogis. Yogi-śara, yatta-yogi-śara-kṛṣṇa. The yogis also, they are deficient with Kṛṣṇa's power. Still, some rascals, without any yoga-siddhi, they claim that I have become God. What is your qualification? Have you got all the yoga-siddha? Then how you claim that you are? But rascals, they claim to become God, and other rascals, they also believe that here is God. Both of them are animals.

### Krishna's Order, Arjuna's Role, Bhagavad-gita's Purpose
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/h8hMfQp6ZFs?t=1456
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "Arjuna is playing like that, how this Bhagavad-gītā will come?"
**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada explains that Arjuna's apparent bewilderment is a deliberate act to facilitate the revelation of Bhagavad-gita for the benefit of the world.

So Kṛṣṇa's order must be final. If He says, then everything is all right. So here Arjuna's position is, Kṛṣṇa has already arranged the battle, and He knows that Kṛṣṇa wants this battle. Still He says, that yadīvāṁ apratīkāraḥ, He decides in His own way, this is karmāyāṁa. He knows what is Kṛṣṇa's desire, and still He is speaking His own philosophy. That means Arjuna is placing himself on the position of ordinary man. Ordinary man does not know what is Kṛṣṇa. And what is Kṛṣṇa's desire. And he manufactures his own philosophy and thoughts. That is ordinary man. But Arjuna, he is always friend of Kṛṣṇa, constant friend. His name is Gurā-keśa, above all darkness. Certainly he must be one who is Kṛṣṇa's friend, directly. How there can be ignorance? There cannot be. Then why Arjuna is playing that part? He knows Kṛṣṇa's desire. Still He says, that yadīvāṁ apratīkāraḥ, asastraṁ śastra-pāṇayaṁ, and nūṁ tan-veṣeṁ ata-raṁ. He is playing like that. Because without playing, Arjuna is playing like that, how this Bhagavad-gītā will come? This is just like, just like playing on the stage. One very rich man, he is in a drama, he is playing the part of a very poor man. But actually he is not poor man. But in the stage he is playing the part of a poor man. Similarly, Arjuna is not builder. But he is playing the part of a poor man. Similarly, Arjuna is not builder. But for the time being he appears to be bewildered by Kṛṣṇa's māyā. Because Kṛṣṇa wants to speak Bhagavad-gītā for the benefit of the whole world. So what is spiritual knowledge?

**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/h8hMfQp6ZFs?t=1613

**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers

**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada explains that all material counteractions are ultimately ineffective without Krishna's sanction, using the example of Prahlada Maharaja.

Therefore this is a stage arrangement. So, prati-kāraṁ and aprati-kāraṁ. So, prati-kāraṁ and aprati-kāraṁ. This whatever we have manufactured, prati-kāraṁ, counteraction, that will be also failure if Kṛṣṇa does not sanction it. That is realized by Prahlāda Mahārāja. He says, my dear Lord, Hīraṇyakāršipu, that people have manufactured so many prati-kāraṁ, counteraction. counteraction. But tanu-vṛtāṁ those who have accepted this material body they are simply manufacturing things to counteract dangers. But even though they have all these counteracting machines or counteracting agents, still without your sanction these counteracting machine or agent will not be fruitful. Similarly Arjuna is being protected by Kṛṣṇa. So even though Arjuna is not well equipped of prati-kāra, still he will be saved. Because Kṛṣṇa is there. tāvat vibhūtaṁ vṛtāṁ tad-peksitāṇā And even one is well equipped and if Kṛṣṇa does not like to save him, he will not be saved. Always mind this. rāke kṛṣṇa māreke māre kṛṣṇa rākeke This is ordinary. If Kṛṣṇa wants to kill you, nobody can save you. And if Kṛṣṇa wants to save you, nobody can kill you. This is the position.

### Krishna's Protection, Surrender, Bhagavad-gita Philosophy
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/h8hMfQp6ZFs?t=1737
**Verse References:** BG 18.66
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers, Newcomers
**Key Quote:** "Real pratikāraṁ is Kṛṣṇa."
**Summary:** Srila Prabhupada concludes by emphasizing that true protection comes from surrendering to Krishna, as taught in Bhagavad-gita.

So the examples I have given by Prahlāda Mahārāja. bāla-śaṇīha-saranaṁ pitarau nṛsiṁha My Lord, Nṛsiṁha-deva, the parents of children, they are not actually protector of the children. Because generally we think that this child, this boy has got his father. Father and mother, he is well protected. No. Their father and mother, every father and mother wants to protect the child, but still the child has to meet some danger and dies. There are so many experiences. Similarly, bāla-śaṇīha-saranaṁ pitarau nṛsiṁha The father and mother is a counteraction for the dangers of the child. But Prahlāda Mahārāja said, no, they are not counteraction. It is not that if a child is in danger, because the father and mother is very strong, very rich, he will be able to give protection to the child. No, that is not possible. Then, nārtyasya-cāgadha The medicine, a person is suffering from some disease, some fatal disease. If you think, I shall engage first class physician and I shall supply first class medicine, if you think then it will be, the patient will be safe. No, that is not possible. That is not possible. We have got many experiences like that. Then, no rich man would have died. Because he has got money, he can employ first class physician, first class medicine, and simply by engaging such things, counteracting, pratikāraṁ. He cannot be safe. There are many examples like that. So the conclusion is, tāvat vibhūtaṁ vṛtāṁ tada pe kṣitānāṁ If you neglect, if you have decided, that this person, this child cannot be safe, then any amount of pratikāraṁ will not help. Will not help. Therefore, real pratikāraṁ is Kṛṣṇa. Real pratikāraṁ is Kṛṣṇa. Counter it. So, better we take shelter of Kṛṣṇa. As Kṛṣṇa says, sarva-dharmān parityajya mām ekaṁ śaraṇaṁ vrajaḥ. You must always know that no counteraction will be beneficial for us unless we are protected by Kṛṣṇa. So therefore, our business is fully surrender to Kṛṣṇa and seek His protection. Kṛṣṇa says, yes, ahaṁ tvā sarva-pāpebhaṁ akṣuṣyaṁ, I shall give you protection. This is Bhagavān's Bhagavad-gītā philosophy. We have to believe on the assertion of Kṛṣṇa that He is prepared to give me all protection provided I have fully surrendered unto His lotus feet. Thank you very much.

### renunciation, devotion, surrender
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/jQgypRuR8Bw?t=148
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** story
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "Raghunath Das' life of austerity and devotion remains eternal."
**Summary:** This segment discusses Raghunath Das Goswami's attempts to renounce, Chaitanya Mahaprabhu's advice, his eventual escape to Puri, and his exemplary devotion.

Despite repeated attempts to leave home for Jagannath Puri to accompany the Lord, he was sent back. Chaitanya Mahaprabhu advised him against false renunciation, Markata Vairagya, urging him to engage in befitting renunciation, Yukta Vairagya. Raghunath Das married as per his parents' wish but remained internally devoted to Lord Chaitanya. Raghunath Das harbored a deep longing to reunite with Lord Gauranga. Ceasing an opportunity to escape, he fled to Puri, surrendering to Lord Chaitanya. In Puri, he exhibited exemplary renunciation, pleasing Mahaprabhu who gifted him Govardhanashila and Gunjamala. Raghunath Das' life of austerity and devotion remains eternal. He is an enduring source of inspiration, epitomizing the essence of surrender and devotion to the Lord. While most cannot imitate his extreme renunciation, his example encourages seekers to cultivate deeper spiritual dedication and humility in their own lives.

## Mahabharata: The History of Greater India | HDG Srila Prabhupada | Bg 2.1 | 05.08.2024
**Speaker:** HDG Srila Prabhupada

### ignorance, compassion, self-realization
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/3AxaWNAZbWU?t=0
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "Compassion for the eternal soul is real self-realization."
**Summary:** This segment focuses on Sanjaya's description of Arjuna's lamentation and Krishna's role in dispelling ignorance through the Bhagavad Gita, emphasizing that true compassion lies in understanding the eternal soul, not the material body.

Om Namo Bhagavate Vasudevaya. In Srimad Bhagavate Gita, Chapter 2, Contained Bhagavate Gita, Summarized, Verse 1, Sanjayo Vacha. Tam Tatha krupaya vishtam, ashrupurna kulekshanam, vishidantam idam vakyam, vacha Madhusudana. Translation in Perpetual Bhai's Divangresh. Translation: Sanjayo said, seeing Arjuna full of compassion and very sorrowful, his eyes brimming with tears, Madhusudana, Krishna, spoke the following words. Perpetual compassion, lamentation, and tears are all signs of ignorance of the real self. Compassion for the eternal soul is real self-realization. The word Madhusudana is significant in this verse. Lord Krishna killed the demon Madhu, and now Arjuna wanted Krishna to kill the demon of misunderstanding that had overtaken him in the discharge of his duty. No one knows where compassion should be applied. Compassion for the dress of a drowning man is senseless. A man fallen in the ocean of nescience cannot be saved simply by rescuing his outward dress, the gross material body. One who does not know this and laments for the outward dress is called a Shudra, or one who laments unnecessarily. Arjuna was a Kshatriya, and this conduct was not expected from him. Lord Krishna, however, can dissipate the lamentation of the ignorant man, and for this purpose the Bhagavad Gita was sung by him. This chapter instructs us in self-realization by an analytical study of the material body and the spirit soul. As explained by the supreme authority, Lord Shri Krishna, this realization is made possible by working with the fruity being situated in the fixed conception of the real self. Thus ends the Bhaktivinoda Purport.

That position is greater than to become one with Kṛṣṇa. So there are five kinds of liberation, sājūrya. The first liberation is supposed to be sājūrya, means to become one with the Supreme. The Māyāvāda philosopher, monist, they aspire after sājūrya-mukti. But the devotees, Vaiṣṇavas, they do not aspire to become one with Kṛṣṇa. They aspire to become one with Kṛṣṇa. The devotee does not approach the Supreme for any material gain. Just pure devotion means without any aspiration of any kind of material gain or even spiritual gain. ### transcendental form, material conception, nirakara
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/3AxaWNAZbWU?t=553
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "When we use this word nirākā, that means He is not anything of this material world."
**Summary:** This segment explains that Krishna, Vishnu, and Narayana are transcendental and not of this material world, clarifying that 'nirakara' means the Lord's form is not material, but He possesses a transcendental form (sac-cid-ananda-vigraha).

And in the Śrīmad-Bhāgavatam also it is said, sabhi-puṁśāṁ paro dharmaḥ. Paro means transcendental. Beyond this material conception, Kṛṣṇa or the Absolute, Nārāyaṇa, that is paro, Nārāyaṇa-paro of bhakti-āyam. Nārāyaṇa is not anything of this material world. Nārāyaṇa, Kṛṣṇa, Viṣṇu, the Absolute Personality of Godhead, He is not anything of this material world. When we use this word nirākā, that means He is not anything of this material world. But He has got His form, that is transcendental form, sac-cid-ānanda-vigrahaḥ. Nirākār means He has no such form as we have got this material form. This material form is neither of the three transcendental bliss, sac-cid-ānanda-vigrahaḥ, this is asat, acit, and nirānanda-vigrahaḥ. This body, this material body is asat, acit, and nirānanda-vigrahaḥ. Therefore when in the Vedic literature on an authorized statement we find nirākār, that means His form does not belong to this asat, acit, or nirānanda-vigrahaḥ.

And there are different sections within each of these four divisions. As in the ocean, there are always different waves, either on the eastern side, the western side, the northern side or the southern side. Most similarly, Bhakti Rasam of the Sindhu… That Bhakti Rasam Brta Sindhu, the Sanskrit word, we have shortcut the translation, Nectar of Devotion, but the Rupa Gosvami's purpose is to present the ocean of Bhakti Rasam. Rasam means mellow, the juice. It is like an ocean. This ocean has limitation, but that is unlimited. Ānandā-buddhi-vardhanam. Caitanya Mahāprabhu said, this ocean is increasing. Now, this material… This material ocean, it has got limit. It cannot increase unlimitedly. That is not possible. Otherwise, how we could build? This house is on the beach. No. It is ordered not to come forward beyond this line. But the spiritual bliss, that ocean, is increasing. Ānandā-buddhi-vardhanam. That is the difference between spiritual bliss and material enjoyment.

### Glorification of Krishna, Literature, Grammatical Efficiency
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/TJTn0IJoxRE?t=1470
**Verse References:** SB 1.5.11
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers, Newcomers
**Key Quote:** "The real thing is how much you are feeling for Kṛṣṇa."
**Summary:** This segment discusses the importance of literature that glorifies Krishna, even if it is not grammatically perfect. It emphasizes that the feeling for Krishna is more important than grammatical efficiency.

That is also stated in the Śrīmad-Bhāgavatam. tad-bhāga-viśargaḥ janatāṁ viplavaḥ yasmin pratiḥ ślokam avad-bhattavi nāmāni naṁ tasya yasvaṁ kitāni yad That type of literature, which is describing Kṛṣṇa, nāmāni anantasya yasvaṁ kitāni yad, yatra, in which, in that literature, where simply there is glorification of the Lord Kṛṣṇa, of the ananta, the Supreme Lord, not dry philosophy, simply jugglery of words. That is garbage. So that, not that kind of literature, any literature, simply, simply trying to describe the glories of the ananta. yasaṁ aṁkit yasaṁ aṁkitāni yad śrīṇanti gāyanti gṛṇanti sādhavaḥ Those who are sādhu, those who are devotees, they hear that literature. They hear that literature. Otherwise, another, the next verse, I forget now, that vāyaśatīrthaṁ. That it is being described as vāyaśatīrthaṁ, uśanti mānasā. So this kind of literature, even it is not properly grammatically correct. tad-vāga-viśabhakaḥ janatāṁ viplaṭhaḥ yasmīṁ pratiḥ ślokam avadhyaḥ That, in writing Sanskrit slow, it requires very high education. It is not like, whatever I write, three lines, one line, and two lines, not. There is some metric system, caṇḍa. So śaita, śukadeva Gosvāmī says, even it is not properly composed, but because there is anantasya, anantasya guṇāne, the glorification of ananta, the Supreme, śrīṇanti gāyanti gṛṇanti sādhavaḥ, those who are sādhus, actually, they accept it. It doesn't matter if there is little grammatical mistake or some poetical discrepancies. There are literary rules and regulations. So śāstra says it doesn't matter even there is not perfectly. Śaṅkarāyāsā also says, nāhi nāhir aṣṭhati duḥkīṁ karaḥ . You cannot be saved by simply grammatical efficiency. The grammatical efficiency is secondary. The real thing is how much you are feeling for Kṛṣṇa. That is one thing.

### Hearing About Krishna, Association of Devotees, Pure Devotees
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/TJTn0IJoxRE?t=1672
**Verse References:** SB 3.25.25, SB 1.2.16

nāmāni nantasya yaśaṁ kītāni yad śrīṇanti gṛṇanti gāyanti sādhavaḥ So śrīṇatāṁ sakataḥ kṛṣṇa. We are not professional, that you come here and beg, then we continue, otherwise we stop. No. Our business is to distribute the glories of the Lord. śravaṇaṁ kīrtanaṁ viṣṇu. Therefore it is recommended. satāṁ prasaṅgād mama-vīrya-saṅgitaṁ. In satsangha, satsangha means the association of the devotees. satāṁ prasaṅgād mama-vīrya-saṅgitaṁ bhavante hṛta-karṇa-rasāyantam. Just contrary to this, avaiṣṇava mukha-gīrṇā-pūta-harī-kathā-mṛtaṁ śravaṇaṁ na kaśvatam. Those who are not Vaiṣṇava, those who are not devotees, one should not hear from them. It is useless. It is useless, waste of time. śravaṇaṁ na kaśvatam sarva-kṣiṣṭo pāyo yathā. Just like milk touched by the lips of a serpent is poison. You cannot say, it is milk, very nice. No. Because it is touched by the lips of the serpent, it is useless. Similarly, as soon as a professional reciter or a avaiṣṇava reciter, without any realization, without being a devotee of the Lord, cites, recites, that should not be heard. That is restricted by śrīnātana-guṣa. avaiṣṇava mukha-gīrṇā-pūta-harī-kathā-mṛtaṁ śravaṇaṁ na kaśvatam. Because you will not derive any benefit. You go on hearing for thousands of years, thousands of years. You still will remain where you are in the beginning. But śrīnātana-guṣa-kṣiṣṭo pāyo yathā. But śrīnātana-guṣa-kṣiṣṭo pāyo yathā. But śrīnātana-guṣa-kṣiṣṭo pāyo yathā. So this kathā, rikathā, kṛṣṇa-kathā should be heard from devotees, in the association of devotees.

### devotional service, spiritual life, varieties of life, impersonalism, enjoyment
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/btisyER8-yY?t=18
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "So bhakti-mārga means that you can understand Kṛṣṇa as He is."
**Summary:** This segment discusses how devotional service elevates one to spiritual life, emphasizing the importance of variety and contrasting it with the impersonalists' desire for zero, arguing that true happiness lies in enjoying spiritual varieties.

The process of devotional service as it is recommended in the Nectar of Devotion will gradually elevate one from the material condition of life to the spiritual status. If you actually enter into some planet where there is varieties of life, then you become satisfied. Otherwise, if you remain only in the sky, nirviseś, nirākār, then you will hanker after where is viseś, where is varieties, where is variety. This is natural. Therefore, śāstra says, ārujya-kṛcchena-karangasya, you can go very high with your aeroplane, but if you don't get any shelter in the sky, then you'll have to come back, as they are doing. They are trying to go to the moon planet, not in the sky. The sky, you can remain in the sky while you are coming back. No. That is not very pleasing. So bhakti-mārga means that bhaktām ām abhijanam jāmāṁ yasya mī tattva-tattvam. You can understand Kṛṣṇa as He is. As He is means He is not a human being like you or me. He is the Supreme Personality of body, sac-cid-ānanda-vigrahaḥ īśvaraḥ paramaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sac-cid-ānanda-vigrahaḥ anādhi rādhi govindaḥ sarva-kāraṇa-kāraṇaḥ. That is understanding of Kṛṣṇa. If we understand Kṛṣṇa as our destiny, ordinary human being, abhijānanti māṁ mṛḍhā mānuseṁ tanum āśritam, then we don't understand Kṛṣṇa. We understand Kṛṣṇa's māyā, not Kṛṣṇa. nāhaṁ sarvasya prakāśya yoga-māyā samābhṛtaḥ. Kṛṣṇa cannot be understood because He is covered by yoga-māyā. He can be understood only by the devotees. So the bhakti-mārga means we want real life, eternal life, and varieties also, आनन्द में व्यास है। आनन्द, variety is the matter of enjoyment. विदाओं वैराइटी, you cannot feel enjoyment. विदाओं वैराइटी, आनन्द में व्यास नहीं हो सकता है। That is not possible. विदाओं वैराइटी, आनन्द में व्यास नहीं हो सकता है। Suppose if I simply give you a lump of flower, will you enjoy? प्रभाव करें तो आप जानेंगे। But the same flower, you make kachori, sंघारा, लुची, पूड़ी and this and that, you'll enjoy. आप जानेंगे। The ingredient is the same. But when it is variety, it is enjoyable. प्रभाव में जानेंगे। लुची और पूड़ी और जानेंगे। आप जानेंगे। Similarly, spiritual varieties, the impersonalists, they are being fed up with these material varieties. प्रभाव में जानेंगे। लुची और पूड़ी और जानेंगे। They want to make it zero, but that will not help us. लुची और पूड़ी और जानेंगे। लुची और जानेंगे। In zero, we cannot be happy, because we are, by nature, we want to enjoy. जीरो, हम नहीं खुश हो सकते हैं। और enjoy means there must be variety. पूड़ी और जानेंगे। इसलिए जानेंगे। The same flower, but you pick up some different varieties of flower and keep it. अह, उसके बारे में बिल्कुल भी चुक करें। Just like Kṛṣṇa Himself is expanding Himself as gopas, as cowherds, boys, as cubs and cows and trees in Vṛndāvana, They are all आनंद्र चिन्मय रस। Explanation of Kṛṣṇa's pleasure potential, राधा कृष्ण प्रणय वृकिति अल्लाधिनि शक्ति रस्मा। कृष्णा is the origin of ब्रह्म. Those who are trying for ब्रह्मशु, here is the point, शुकृते घृष्णा, इत्थं ब्रह्म, शुखानु भृत्या, the origin, ब्रह्मणा हंग प्रतिष्ठा, इंपर्शनल ब्रह्म is situated on me, जस्यप्रभाप्रभवतो जगदन्य कोठी, so we get information. So we have to realize these things, what is कृष्णा, that मनुषानाम सहास्तेशु कच्चि जतति सिद्धाम, जतताम भी सिद्धानाम कच्चि वित्ति मांततु. To understand कृष्णा is not very easy thing, मनुषानाम सहास्तेशु. Out of many, many millions who are trying to become successful in the mission of life, मनुषानाम सहास्तेशु कच्चि जतति सिद्धाये, सिद्धाये, सिद्धाये means to become, सिद्धा, means to become ब्रह्म भूत, to understand that I am not this material body, I am ब्रह्मास्तेशु, that is सिद्धि. So out of many शास्तेशु, सिद्धास्तेशु, we have realized पर्मात्मा or ब्रह्मा, out of many such millions of people, one can understand कृष्णा. कृष्णा is so difficult subject matter. But he is so kind also that he is giving us instruction personally in the form of भगवत गीता, what he is, what he is. My dear Arjuna, don't labor hard simply that there is something beyond me. Sometimes they say that there is still more beyond कृष्णा, but कृष्णा says, no, there is nothing beyond, मत्तः परतरः नान्या किंचि जस्ति धनन्या। शुत्रे गणायिव, everything is resting on me. अहं सर्वश्य प्रभुगत। The Vedanta says, जन्मा दस्य जताँ। जन्मा स्थिते लौज। Where it is staying, where it is being conducted, that is Brahman. कृष्णा answers this question that अहं सर्वश्य प्रभुगत। He is deceiving Brahman. Therefore Arjuna accepted him. परंब्रम्म परंधम्। We are Brahmas, but we are not परंब्रम्म। परंब्रम्म is Kṛṣṇa. We are आत्मा, but we are not परंब्रम्मात्मा। परंब्रम्मात्मा is Kṛṣṇa. So in this way, मनुष्चा नाम सहर्षेशु कष्चि जतति सिद्धये जततामपि सिद्ध्यान। कष्चि वेत्ति माम। So in this way, we have to understand Kṛṣṇa. Thank you very much.

### parampara, guru, Krishna's representative, surrender
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/btisyER8-yY?t=621
**Verse References:** —
**Content Type:** philosophy
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers
**Key Quote:** "We have to understand Kṛṣṇa through the paramparā disciple succession, not by our ABCD knowledge."
**Summary:** This segment emphasizes the importance of understanding Kṛṣṇa through the paramparā system, accepting a bona fide spiritual master as Kṛṣṇa's representative, and pleasing him to please Kṛṣṇa.

एमं परंप्राप्रात्म एमं राजर्षय विदु। We have to understand Kṛṣṇa through the paramparā disciple succession, not by our ABCD knowledge. That is not possible. One has to accept the disciple succession line. तद्विज्ञान अर्थम्सव गुरुमेव भिगच्छे। That guru, guru means Kṛṣṇa's representative. शाक्षा धरित्तेन, because guru is representative of Kṛṣṇa. Therefore he should be respected as guru, as Kṛṣṇa. किन्तु प्रवोर्ज्य प्रिय एवत सद्धित्यों। But because a guru is respected as Kṛṣṇa, the guru does not think that he has become Kṛṣṇa. No. That is foolishness. He is the most confidential servant of Kṛṣṇa. Therefore, just like most confidential secretary, he acts as the master. His signature, his settlement, he'll be accepted by the master. Similarly, yasya prasādād bhagavata-prasād. Yasya prasādād naga-tī-pṛto. We are to select the right representative of Kṛṣṇa and accept Him as guru. And if I please Him, then Kṛṣṇa will be pleased. There is no need of somebody, they say that Kṛṣṇa is not present, how shall I please Him? No. Kṛṣṇa's representative is present. You please Him. जस्व देवे पराभक्ति जथा देवे तथा गुरोगुरु। This is the process. आदु गुर्भास्रम्। That is Gosvāmī, Rūpa Gosvāmī giving his, in the Bhakti-rasāmṛta-kṛṣṇa, आदु गुर्भास्रम्. If you are actually interested to understand Kṛṣṇa and Kṛṣṇa-bhakti, the first business is आदु गुर्भास्रम्. You take shelter of a bona fide spiritual master who is representative of Kṛṣṇa. And how we can understand? The representative of Kṛṣṇa. And that is not very difficult, because what Kṛṣṇa says, if the representative says the same thing, then he is representative. It is not very difficult. If his representative says that he surrendered to Kṛṣṇa, he is representative. He does not become himself Kṛṣṇa. That is bogus. A faithful servant will never say that आम ने मास्ता है। I am servant, although he is as good as the master. He is the most confidential ruse.

---
### surrender, Krishna consciousness, chanting, contamination
**Timestamp:** https://youtu.be/btisyER8-yY?t=2367
**Verse References:** BG 18.66
**Content Type:** practical
**Audience:** Full-time devotees, Congregation / volunteers, Newcomers
**Key Quote:** "So this Kṛṣṇa consciousness movement is teaching people to become Kṛṣṇa conscious, means Kṛṣṇa says man-manā bhava mad-bhakto mad-yājī māṁ namaskuru, the four things."
**Summary:** This segment explains that a true guru will always direct one to surrender to Krishna, emphasizing the importance of Krishna consciousness, chanting Hare Krishna, and becoming free from material contamination to return to Godhead.

गुरु, कृष्णा, and the latest गुरु, कृष्णा, because the aim is the same. कृष्णा personally says शर्वधर्मान पुरित्त जम्मामिकं शरुणं भज़ाँ, and who is representative of कृष्णा, he will say the same thing. You surrender to कृष्णा. कृष्णा says मन्मना भवमत भक्त मत जाजि माग नमस्कुरू, the guru will say, yes, you become always कृष्णा conscious. मन्मना. कृष्णा says मन्मना. A guru says you become कृष्णा conscious. The same thing. There is no difference. You become devotee of कृष्णा. You always think of कृष्णा. You always chant of कृष्णा. You always speak of कृष्णा. You do not know anything but कृष्णा. Simply this life is required. So this कृष्णा consciousness movement is teaching people to become कृष्णा, कृष्णा conscious means कृष्णा says मन्मना भव मत भक्त मत जाजि माग नमस्कुरू, the four things. You just become always thinking of कृष्णा. You just become a devotee of कृष्णा. You just offer your obeisances unto कृष्णा and you just worship कृष्णा. And accept कृष्णा, giving up any other engagement. Because real धर्म is to surrender to कृष्णा. Otherwise why कृष्णा says सर्वधर्माल पुरितर्यु. Why he says give up all other so called धर्मास. They are not धर्मास. The cheating type of धर्म is kicked out from this भागवात. Cheating type. Real धर्म, what is that? This is real धर्म. So we request everyone. It is very scientific. It is authorized. We are not talking nonsense. Authorized. We are taking the version of कृष्णा. We are taking the version of the वेदि कंक्रूशन्त्. वेदा, study of वेदा means to understand कृष्णा. One who does not understand कृष्णा, he is simply wasting his time. You can execute your धर्म, your occupational duty, very nicely. That's all right. But if you do not develop कृष्ण consciousness, you are simply wasting your time and working hard for nothing. This is the part. So this कृष्ण consciousness movement is very genuine and it is very easy, especially in this age. That is also authorized statement of Śrūadeva Gosvāmī. He has described, because in this age, in this age it is called कलीजूप। There are so many impediments. People are fallen. They are disturbed. So many botheration. It is very difficult to realize कृष्ण consciousness. But there is very shortcut way recommended. Simply by chanting हरे कृष्ण हरे कृष्ण कृष्ण कृष्ण हरे हरे। You become uncontaminated of this material contamination. And thus being free from material contamination, you become eligible to go back to home, back to God. Thank you very much.
